i need this image on my wall is there an image credit btw nailed it this depends on the particular skills business types with no open source experience are often terrible when they are in a position of authority over open source developers the profit model is entirely different and apparently incomprehensible unless they ve either seen it up close or have very carefully studied e g cygnus and rhat business models i spent a few years in the mid is working on the design of fault tolerant organizations hoping to create information exchange pathways inside organizations that limited the harm that could be done through the loss or failure of any individual the large scale experiment the scaleable company that we were building pretty much failed ended up being rebuilt form the ground up on a different basis using contractor labor in part because i had neither identified nor solved these problems and in part because we were working inside an existing organizational structure and not all the systems for necessary decentralization and elimination of single points of failure could be implemented as much as the article is text the image you chose to illustrate it speaks to the most interesting approach to this problem i have seen anyone take to date about years ago a good friend was running a nonprofit with a chronically dysfunctional board of directors he gained access to a big
